if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'b5bc0e72c7e3aa61d889a39389205e59a4d1889a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'b5bc0e72c7e3aa61d889a39389205e59a4d1889a') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'de66b8dd4d8349dbdaf6c39789f9eda77e040c62') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'b5bc0e72c7e3aa61d889a39389205e59a4d1889a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_6();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') != '0218c90a13fbbc6a6af145fabff0ada19c2ccdf5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== '0218c90a13fbbc6a6af145fabff0ada19c2ccdf5') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== 'e6500c587ef2be13ec8e3d1c892844b9542dedf2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php') !== '0218c90a13fbbc6a6af145fabff0ada19c2ccdf5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/webwhois.php');
		}
	}
